      if (!window.P) {window.P = window.ASPP;}

      
      
      if (!P.guardFatal) {
        P.guardFatal = function (name, callback) {
          if ( !callback ) {
            callback = name;
            name = undefined;
          }

          var join = function(delimiter, a, b, c) {
            var firstTwo = a &amp;&amp; b ? a + delimiter + b : a || b;
            return c ? join(delimiter, firstTwo, c) : firstTwo;
          };

          return function guarded () {
            try {
              var result = callback.apply(this, arguments);
              return result;
            }
            catch (err) {
              var console = window.console;
              if (console &amp;&amp; console.error) {
                console.error(join(String.fromCharCode(10),
                  join(": ", name, err.message),
                  err.stack || err
                ));
              }
            }
          };
        }
      }

    P.register('sc-widget-strings', function() {
        
        return {
            collapse: '\u6298\u53E0',
            expand: '\u5C55\u5F00'
        };
    });

    P.when('jQuery').execute('register-widget-events', function($) {
        var widgetIdPrefix = 'widget-';
        $(".gw-cont").find("div[id^=" + widgetIdPrefix + "]").each(function () {
            try {
                var widgetEvt = 'dashiell-widget-' + $(this).attr('id').substring(widgetIdPrefix.length) + '-jsp-rendered';
                P.register(widgetEvt, function () {return true;});
            } catch (exception) {
                if (window.ueLogError) {
                    var additionalInfo = {
                        logLevel : 'FATAL',
                        attribution : 'scgateway:dashiell_widget_registration',
                        message : exception.message
                    };
                    window.ueLogError(exception,additionalInfo);
                    console.error('Exception occurred while registering widget: ' + exception.message);
                }
            }

        });
    });

    P.when('jQuery').execute('register-kpi-events', function($) {
        $('.kpiFlexItem .kpiSummaryContent').each(function () {
            var kpiEvent = 'scgateway-' + $(this).attr('id') ;
            P.register(kpiEvent, function () {return true;});
        });
    });

    
    P.when('A', 'sc-gateway-insert-cards').execute('sc-ready-r2s2_fnFbrJ', function(A) {

            var firstTwo = a &amp;&amp; b ? a + delimiter + b : a || b;

<script type="text/javascript">
    (function(){
    document.getElementById("myo-hmd").addEventListener("click", function(event){
        var hmdTab = document.getElementById('hmd2-trigger-tab');
            if(hmdTab){
                var hmdLink = hmdTab.getElementsByTagName('a');
                if (hmdLink[0]){
                    hmdLink[0].click();
                }
            }
        event.preventDefault();
    })})();
</script>

        P.guardFatal = function (name, callback) {
          if ( !callback ) {
            callback = name;
            name = undefined;
          }

          var join = function(delimiter, a, b, c) {
            var firstTwo = a &amp;&amp; b ? a + delimiter + b : a || b;
            return c ? join(delimiter, firstTwo, c) : firstTwo;
          };

          return function guarded () {
            try {
              var result = callback.apply(this, arguments);
              return result;

                  err.stack || err

    (function(){
    document.getElementById("myo-hmd").addEventListener("click", function(event){
        var hmdTab = document.getElementById('hmd2-trigger-tab');
            if(hmdTab){
                var hmdLink = hmdTab.getElementsByTagName('a');
                if (hmdLink[0]){
                    hmdLink[0].click();
                }
            }
        event.preventDefault();
    })})();
</script>

      if (!P.guardFatal) {
        P.guardFatal = function (name, callback) {
          if ( !callback ) {
            callback = name;
            name = undefined;
          }

          var join = function(delimiter, a, b, c) {
            var firstTwo = a &amp;&amp; b ? a + delimiter + b : a || b;
            return c ? join(delimiter, firstTwo, c) : firstTwo;
          };

          return function guarded () {
            try {
              var result = callback.apply(this, arguments);
              return result;
            }
            catch (err) {
              var console = window.console;
              if (console &amp;&amp; console.error) {
                console.error(join(String.fromCharCode(10),
                  join(": ", name, err.message),
                  err.stack || err
                ));
              }
            }
          };

      if (!window.P) {window.P = window.ASPP;}

      
      
      if (!P.guardFatal) {
        P.guardFatal = function (name, callback) {
          if ( !callback ) {
            callback = name;
            name = undefined;
          }

          var join = function(delimiter, a, b, c) {
            var firstTwo = a &amp;&amp; b ? a + delimiter + b : a || b;
            return c ? join(delimiter, firstTwo, c) : firstTwo;
          };

          return function guarded () {
            try {
              var result = callback.apply(this, arguments);
              return result;
            }
            catch (err) {
              var console = window.console;
              if (console &amp;&amp; console.error) {
                console.error(join(String.fromCharCode(10),
                  join(": ", name, err.message),
                  err.stack || err
                ));
              }
            }
          };
        }
      }

    (function(){
    document.getElementById("myo-hmd").addEventListener("click", function(event){
        var hmdTab = document.getElementById('hmd2-trigger-tab');
            if(hmdTab){
                var hmdLink = hmdTab.getElementsByTagName('a');
                if (hmdLink[0]){
                    hmdLink[0].click();
                }
            }
        event.preventDefault();
    })})();
